# Redrob — Candidates to Label

Read each card (~30s). Fill in `eval/labels.csv` with one row per `candidate_id`.

**Tier scale (against JD):** 0 honeypot · 1 clear no · 2 weak · 3 maybe · 4 strong · 5 ideal

**Touchstone:** *if you had this candidate and only this JD, would you forward them to the hiring manager?* → tier 4+. *Worth a call but not forward?* → tier 3.

---
